z=z(j,k(k,k),k(k,k));k(1);return z;end;end;end else if 7>k then do return e[j]end;else if k>7 then do return j(k,nil,j);end else do return setmetatable({},{['__\99\97\108\108']=function(k,e,r,j,z)if z then return k[z]elseif j then return k else k[e]=r end end})end end end end end end),...)
